style=\"font-size:14px;text-decoration-line:underline;\"> 2017 from 10:00am to 2:00pm</span><span style=\"font-size:14px;\"> at </span><span lang=\"EN-CA\" style=\"font-size:14px;text-decoration-line:underline;\">GFK School in Carlyle</span><span style=\"font-size:14px;\">, SK.</span><span style=\"font-size:14px;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"font-size:14px;\">There will be presentations on the Power Engineering 20 and 30 courses that are available to our SECPSD students in the 2017-2018 as part of our partnership with Sask. Power and Prairie South School Division.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-size:14px;\"></span><span style=\"font-size:14px;\">&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-size:14px;\">T</span><span style=\"font-size:14px;\">here will also be representatives from South East Regional College, Sask. Polytechnic, and Sask. Power</span><span style=\"font-size:14px;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"font-size:14px;\">to present information on related occupational fields such as Industrial Mechanics, and Chemical Technology.</span></p><p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; As part of the Career Spotlight, students will also receive a tour of the Sask. Power Mobile Power Lab that will be stationed at GFK School in Carlyle, SK.&nbsp; This lab is an exciting hands-on practical learning component of the Power Engineering 20 and 30 courses. </p><p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The Power Engineering Career Spotlight is open to any <span lang=\"EN-CA\" style=\"text-decoration:underline;\">current Grade 10 and 11</span> South East Cornerstone students. Transportation to and from the Career Spotlight in Carlyle is the responsibility of the students/parents and all participants are asked to bring a lunch with them that day. &nbsp;Registration form is <a href=\"/group/3yz7y89/Lists/SharedDocuments/Spotlight%20on%20Pwr%20Eng%202017%20-%20Student%20Info%20and%20Reg%20Form.docx?Web=1\">here</a></p></div></span></div>\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div
